\DoxyCodeLine{59 \textcolor{comment}{/* glcorearb.h is for use with OpenGL core profile implementations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{60 \textcolor{comment}{** It should should be placed in the same directory as gl.h and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{61 \textcolor{comment}{** included as <GL/glcorearb.h>.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{62 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{63 \textcolor{comment}{** glcorearb.h includes only APIs in the latest OpenGL core profile}}
\DoxyCodeLine{64 \textcolor{comment}{** implementation together with APIs in newer ARB extensions which }}
\DoxyCodeLine{65 \textcolor{comment}{** can be supported by the core profile. It does not, and never will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{66 \textcolor{comment}{** include functionality removed from the core profile, such as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{67 \textcolor{comment}{** fixed-\/function vertex and fragment processing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{68 \textcolor{comment}{**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{69 \textcolor{comment}{** Do not \#include both <GL/glcorearb.h> and either of <GL/gl.h> or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{70 \textcolor{comment}{** <GL/glext.h> in the same source file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{71 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{72 }
